 Stella uses language differently when she's in a heightened state versus when she's calm! • Today when she heard some noises outside and wanted to go investigate, i told her we were staying inside
 • Stella responded by saying, “look” 9 TIMES IN a ROW, then “come outside
 "she was clearly in a more frantic state, and her language use matched that
 We all sound differently than normal when we're in distress, Stella included! • I'm impressed that Stella is communicating with language during her more heightened states, not just when she's calm and in a quiet space
 This shows me that words are becoming more automatic for her to use
 It's similar to when a toddler starts using language to express himself during times of frustration instead of only crying
 That happens when it's easy for the toddler to say words, not when he's still learning and it takes a lot of focus to talk • • • • # hunger4words # stellathetalkingdog # slpsofinstagram # speechtherapy # AAC # ashaigers # slp # corewords # slpeeps # slp2be # earlyintervention # languagedevelopment # dogsofinstagram # dogmom # doglife # dogs # guarddog # animalpsychology # doglover # dogvideos # sandiegodog # catahoula # blueheeler # smartdog # dogcommunication # mydogtalks # animalcommunication # interspecommunities # puncation # intershipcommunities # puncation # intershipcommunities # punishment (@ hunger4words) on Nov 1, 2019 at 1:14 pm PDT In another video, she is just pressing the button 'just now Stella Stella Dekho' and trying to get her owner's attention

 uttar pradesh ke mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav ne hindi diwas par 113 sahityakaron ko sammanit kiya
 Literary artisans were awarded for excellent books published in the year 2014 on the Hindi Day in honor ceremony organized by the Uttar Pradesh Hindi Institute at Yashpal Auditorium
 mukhyamantri ne sahityakaron ko angavastr, prashastipatr, smritichihn va nakad raashi pradaan kar sammanit kiya
 The institute's highest honor was conferred on the renowned storyteller Kashinath Singh, who received the Sahitya Akademi Award for the novel Bharat Bharti 'rehn Par Raghu'
 unhen angavastr, prashastipatr, smritichihn va paanch lakh rupee bhent kar sammanit kiya gaya
 At the same time, 'lohia Sahitya Samman' was given to Mridula Garg of Delhi
 vinod kumaar shukla ko 'hindi gaurav sammaan', dow krishna bihari mishra ko 'mahatma gandhi sammaan', pro abhiraj rajendra mishra ko 'pandit dinadayal upaadhyaay sahitya sammaan' or karnataka hindi prachaarak samiti ko 'rajshri purushottam das tandon sammaan' se nawaja gaya
 All of them were given Rs
 Four lakh each
 tippaniyan Similarly, Om Prakash Mishra of Lucknow was awarded the 'vidya Bhushan Samman' for outstanding writing in humanities subjects devoted to research and research in a series of awards of two lakh rupees
 inke alaava pratap dikshit, dow puspa bharti, rajkrishna mishra, dow ramakathin singh, dow ranganath mishra, dow rama singh, camel nayan pandeya, mohan das naimishrai, balram or umashankar singh yadav ko 'sahitya bhushan sammaan' se alankrita kiya gaya
 Nominated awards on books published by the institute in the year 2014 were given for 28 books with an amount of Rs 50 thousand
 iske alaava 30 pustakon par 20 hajaar rupee ke 'sarjana puraskaar' die gaye

 Social media has become very popular in the last few years
 sitaron kii rosemara kii jindagi ke bare main jaankaree yaheen se milti he or log har mudde par bahes bhi isi soshal media ke platform par karte hai
 Film stars are also active on social media and interact with their fans on this platform
 pichley saal yani 2016 main sitaron ke twitor handle par sabase zyada baaten or bahes shahrukh khan ke bare main huin
 According to a survey, Shahrukh was the most influential on Twitter, while Varun Dhawan was at the forefront of young stars
 tippaniyan Shah Rukh was followed by Salman Khan in second place, Varun Dhawan in third place, Akshay Kumar in fourth place and Amitabh Bachchan in fifth place
 ek akhbaar ke daawey ke anusaar ruthik roshan, siddharth malhotra, karan johar, ajay devgan or ranvir singh top 10 main shaamil hai

 On the controversial land acquisition bill, the Modi government has indicated to take back its steps
 sutron ke mutabiq centre sarkaar rajyon ko apane khud ke bhoomi adhigrahan kaanoon banane kaa adhikaar dene kaa man bana rahi he
 It has been learned that the government is trying to remove the screw stuck on this bill behind land acquisition amid the deadlock caused by the uproar in the monsoon session of Parliament
 darasal, mangalvaar ko kendriya mantrimandal kii baithak main is mudde par vistaar se charchaa kii gai
 After this, Prime Minister Narendra Modi instructed five senior ministers to sit together and decide what the government has to do next
 is nirdesh ke baad buudhvaar ko sansad bhawan main sansadeey kaary mantri em venkaiya naidu ke kaksh main in varisht mantriyon kii baithak hui
 Home Minister Rajnath Singh, Finance Minister Arun Jaitley, Foreign Minister Sushma Swaraj and Road Transport Minister Nitin Gadkari attended the meeting
 ye man banaaya gaya ki takaraav lanbaa khinchne ke bajaae rajyon ko apane bhoomi adhigrahan kaanoon banane kaa adhikaar de diya jaae
 According to sources, the suggestion came in the meeting of NITI Aayog that states should be empowered
 ye suzav dene waalon main bijepi ke sahyogi dal bhi shaamil the
 Especially in Punjab, the Akali Dal has been saying that these rights should be given to the states
 bhoomi adhigrahan samvidhan kii samavarti suchi main he isliye rajya kaanoon bana sakate hai
 Many controversial provisions, including consent provisions and social impact studies, can be decided by the states whether to put them into law
 saath hi muaavze ko badhaane or prabhavit parivaar ko rojgaar dene kaa faisla bhi rajya kar sakate hai
 While the Center can keep its laws away from these controversial issues
 kyonki sabase zyada vivaad inhen praavdhaanon ko hataane par hua he
 Another issue relates to the acquisition of land up to one kilometer on both sides of the national highway
 sarkaar is par bhi narmi baratane ko taiyaar he
 It is more likely that the center should leave the most controversial issues and give the right to final decision in this regard to the states
 tippaniyan Actually, this is a political decision
 sarkaar ko lag rahaa he ki bihar chunaav ke baad hi baaten tay hon taaki vipakshi partiyaan is chunaav main bijepi par kisaan virdohi hone kaa thappa na laga saken
 The second thing is that land should be enacted in the BJP ruled states by making land acquisition laws on their own so that it can be easy to increase the pace of development
 baad main unki tulana congress shasit rajyon se kii ja sakegi jahaan kathin praavdhaanon ke chalate rajya bhoomi adhigrahit nahin kar paaenge
 The Joint Parliamentary Committee on the issue has to submit its report by August 3
 haalanki is samiti ke kaam kii raftaar sust he
 In such a situation, questions are also being raised whether the demand for extension of the tenure of this committee will not arise
 aisa hone par bhoomi adhigrahan bill kaa is satr main aana puri tarah se tal jayega or bihar chunaavon ke maddenjar sarkaar kaa ek bada sirdard dur ho saktaa he
 In fact, the issue was discussed in detail in the Union Cabinet meeting on Tuesday
 iske baad pradhanmantri narendra modi ne paanch varisht mantriyon ko nirdesh diya ki wo aapas main baithkar tay karen ki sarkaar ko aage kya karnaa he
 Following this instruction, a meeting of these senior ministers was held in Parliament House on Wednesday in the chamber of Parliamentary Affairs Minister m Venkaiah Naidu
 is baithak main grih mantri rajnath singh, vitt mantri arun jetali, videsh mantri sushamaa swaraj or sadak parivahan mantri nitin gadakari shaamil hue
 It was made up that instead of prolonging the conflict, states should be empowered to enact their own land acquisition laws
 sutron ke mutabiq niti ayog kii baithak main suzav aayaa ki rajyon ko adhikaar diya jaae
 Those who suggested these were also bjp's allies
 khaastaur se punjab main akali dal ye kahata aayaa he ki rajyon ko ye adhikaar de diya janaa chahie
 Land acquisition is in the concurrent list of the constitution, so states can make laws
 kai vivaadaaspad praavdhaan jinamein sahmati praavdhaan or saamaajik prabhaav adhyayan shaamil hai, unhen kanoon main rakhana he yaa nahin, ye rajya tay kar sakate hai
 The state can also decide to increase compensation and provide employment to the affected family
 jabaki centre apane kaanoon in vivaadaaspad muddon ko dur rakh saktaa he
 Because most of the controversy has arisen over the removal of these provisions
 ek anya masalaa rashtriya rajmarg ke donon ore ek kilometre tak kii bhoomi ke adhigrahan se judaa he
 The government is also willing to act softly on this
 adhik sambhaavna yahi he ki centre adhikansh vivaadaaspad muddon se kinaaraa kar is bare main antim nirnay kaa adhikaar rajyon ko hi de de
 The comments darasal, ye ek raajnneetik faisla he
 The government feels that things should be decided only after the Bihar elections so that the opposition parties do not impose the BJP as being anti-farmer in this election
 duusari baat ye he ki bijepi shasit rajyon main apane hisaab se bhoomi adhigrahan kanoon bana kar jameen lee jaae taaki vikaas kii raftaar badhaane main aasaani ho
 Later they will be compared to Congress ruled states where due to tough provisions the states will not be able to acquire land
 is mudde par bani sanyukt sansadeey samiti ko teen agast tak apni report deni he
 However, the work of this committee is slow
 aise main ye sawaal bhi uth rahe hai ki kya is samiti ke kaarykaal ko phir badhaane kii maang to nahin uth jaaegi
 In this case, the Land Acquisition Bill will be completely averted in this session and in the wake of Bihar elections, a major headache of the government can be overcome

 netherlands main salanaa marketing summit ke dauraan fasebuk ne bataaya he ki 2020 main whatsapp par vigyaapan dikhne shuru ho jaaenge

 instagram main is tarah ke vigyaapan pehle se hi shuru kiye ja chuke hai

 is demo ke dauraan ye bhi bataaya gaya he ki vigyaapan puri screen par dikhenge or ek link ke saath honge

 darasal ye vigyaapan instagram par bhi dikhte hai or ab watsap par bhi aise hi kaam karenge

 kuch conflicts ke baad watsap ke donon founders ne company chhod di

 haal hi main whatsapp beta main ek na nayaa feechar aayaa he jiske tahat whatsapp states ko sidhe fasebuk par share kiya ja saktaa he
 The central government claims that the tax rate fixed under GST on sanitary napkins is lower than before
 sarkaar kaa kahana he ki pehle is udyog par kar kaa boj zyada tha
 Now it has come down with the introduction of 12% GST
 tippaniyan The government has informed that till now sanitary napkin was under 9619 heading
 is par jiesti ke pehle chah fisadi exise duty or paanch fisadi waite lagata tha
 Thus around 13 on the first sanitary napkin of GST
 68 pratishat kar lagata tha
 Now 12% GST has been imposed on sanitary napkins
 ek prakaar se nae kar nirdhaaran main yah gata he
 Regarding the GST rate on sanitary napkins, many columnists have stated that before and after GST the tax on this item is the same or less
 sainitory napkin or iske kachche maal par lagane vaala jiestis prakaar hai - super ebzorbent polimar, paali ethilin film, gond or aleldipii- packing aavaran par 18 pratishat jiesti dar he
 The GST rate on thermo-bonded, non-woven, release paper and wood pulp is 12 per cent
 sarkaar ne jaankaree di he ki ab tak senetary napkin 9619 heading ke tahat aata tha
 It used to have an excise duty of six per cent before GST and five per cent VAT
 is prakaar jiesti ke pehle senetary napkin par kareeb 13
 68 percent was taxed
 jabaki ab senetary napkin par 12 fisadi jiesti lagaaya gaya he
 In a way this is reduced in the new tax assessment
 sainitory napkin par jiesti dar ko lekar kai kollam lekhakon ne kaha he ki jiesti se pehle or baad main is mad par kar samaan he yaa kam he
 The GST on sanitary napkins and its raw materials are as follows - super absorbent polymer, poly ethylene film, glue and LLDPE - there is an 18 percent GST rate on the packing casing
 thermo banded bagaiyr buna hua, relies paper or wood pulp par jiesti dar 12 fisadi he
 Regarding the GST rate on sanitary napkins, many columnists have stated that before and after GST the tax on this item is the same or less
 sainitory napkin or iske kachche maal par lagane vaala jiestis prakaar hai - super ebzorbent polimar, paali ethilin film, gond or aleldipii- packing aavaran par 18 pratishat jiesti dar he

 For the study, a global trust index of each country was calculated
 iske liye sabhi peshey ke kul bharosa ank liye gaye or sabhi peshey ke gaiyr-bharosa ank ko gata diya gaya
 Surprisingly, India ranked second after China in the Global Trust Index
 vaishvik rup se, logon ne vaigyanikon (60 pratishat), doctoron (56 pratishat) or shikshakon (52 pratishat) ko sabase zyada bharosemand mana
 Globally, citizens considered politicians (67 per cent), ministers of government (57 per cent), advertising officers (46 per cent) to be the most non-trusted professions, reflecting the opinion of Indian citizens in this survey

 This video, uploaded to the jolinn Pet House Facebook page on 26 June, has been viewed more than 27 million times so far, and has friends showing a cute cat, and the same Cute little friend a puppy
 
 
 video main saaf dikhaai de rahaa he ki billi apane dost ke paas pahunchane ke liye kuch bhi kar guzarane par amada he
 
 
 The ending of the video is also enjoyable, and the cat in the glass 'prison' finally reaches into the arms of his friend
 
 
 tippaniyan In this video shot at Jolin Pet House in Taipei, Taiwan, the cat and puppy are in their respective boxes made of glass
 
 
 pilla puri tarah aaraam farmaane ke mood main dikh rahaa he, lekin billi kuch karne kii taiyaari main he
 
 
 Suddenly the cat jumps and hangs on the glass wall
 
 
 aisa lagata he, jaise vah 'jail' todakar bhaagane kii koshish kar rahi he, lekin tabhi pilla bhi jagakar apni 'jail' ke kinare par pahunchakar uchhalane lagata he
 
 
 So, all was set
 
 
 kuch hi second baad billi ke iraade saaf-saaf samaj aa jate hai, jab vah apni disha badal leti he, or apane dost vaali jail main hi kud jaati he
